 nepal televijan (antivi) ne 'tito satya' naamak kaarykram ke ek bhaag kaa prasaaran karne par roak laga di

 unka kahana he ki isamen kuch hisson ko sampadit kiya janaa he

 baat yah he ki sampadakeey team ek chote hisse ko sampadit karnaa chaahati thi or samay ke abhaav ke kaaran kaarykram ke is bhaag ko prasaaran se waapas le liya gaya

 Sunrisers Hyderabad beat defending champions Kolkata Knight Riders by 16 runs by Duckworth Lewis Rules in the 19th match of rain-interrupted IPL-8 at the YS Rajasekhara Reddy ACA VDCA Stadium on Wednesday, thanks to the unbeaten innings of captain David Warner (91)
 sunrisers ne pehle ballebaaji karte hue puure 20 over khelkar chaar wicket par 176 ran banaae, lekin barish ke kaaran nite rides ko 12 overon main 118 ranon kaa sanshodhit lakshya mila
 The Knight Riders, however, managed to score 101 runs after losing four wickets in the scheduled overs
 sunrisers kii ipel-8 main ab tak khele paanch maichon main yah duusari jeet he
 With this victory, the Sunrisers moved up to fourth place in the points table, while the Knight Riders remained in third place after scoring six points from three wins in five matches
 nite rides ke liye robin uthppa (34) or manish pandeya (33) hi thodaa sangharsh kar sake
 Captain Gautam Gambhir became clean bowled by Praveen Kumar for just four runs
 lagaataar antaraal par girte viketon ke bich nite rides kabhi bhi ran gati nahin badha sake
 The victory was expected with Andre Russell (19), but after his short innings in 10 balls with a four and a six, the Knight Riders' run rate slowed again and the victory seemed to slip away from his hand
 nite rides aakhri ke chaar overon main maatr 27 ran jod sake
 Sunrisers Hyderabad scored a challenging score of 176 runs in 20 overs thanks to the innings of Warner and Shikhar Dhawan (54)
 warner or dhawan ke bich pehle wicket ke liye 14
 130 runs were scored in 2 overs
 warner ne 55 gendon kii pari main nau chauke or chaar chakke lagaae
 This is his third half-century in this edition of the IPL
 dakshin africa gendbaaj morne morkal ne unhen wicket ke peeche robin uthppa ke haathon kaich karaayaa
 However, the rest of the batsmen could not take advantage of a good start after Warner was dismissed
 duusare wicket ke rup main ravi bopaara (2) kaa bhi wicket morkal ne hasil kiya
 After this, Dhawan was also caught out by Andre Russell in an effort to get a quick run
 dhawan ne 46 gendon kii pari main chaar chauke or ek chakka lagaaya
 The comments naman ojha ne aath gendon main do chhakkon or ek chauke kii madad se 18 ran banaae tathaa chauthe ballebaaj ke rup main pavilion laute
 Sunrisers could add just 47 runs in the last 34 balls after Warner returned to the pavilion
 nite rides kii ore se morkal ko do safalataa mili

 '' In Jind, Haryana, a case of obscene MMS of his own teacher by students studying tuition has come to light
 peedit shikshika ke abhibhavakon dwaara maamle kii shikaayat shahar thana police ko di gai he
 On the complaint of the parents of the teacher, the police have named four students and registered a case against them under various sections and started investigating
 shikshika ne shahar thana police ko di shikaayat main bataaya ki uske paas tarun, varun, rahul va dhairya tution padhane aayaa karte the
 The teacher alleged that when she was alone at home, the four started bullying her
 isi dauraan uskaa ashleel ms bhi banaaya
 Through this MMS, the four youths were also blackmailing him
 jab usne chaaron kaa virodh kiya to unhone ashleel ms anya mobile par dispale kar diya or use jaan se maarane kii dhamkee bhi di
 Station in-charge Kamaldeep said that the matter of making pornographic MMS of the teacher by the students has come to their notice
 unhone peedita ke abhibhavakon kii shikaayat par chaar yuvakon ko namjad kiya he
 The police have started investigating the case by registering a case against the four under various sections
